¶how land englond fyrst named albyon encheson named noble land sirrie ther noble kyng myghty man grete renōme callid dioclisian well worthely hym gouerned ruled thurgh noble chyualrye cōquerd londes hym almost al kynges world entendant hit befel thus dyoclisian spoused gentil damisel wōder fayr emes doughter labana loued hym reson wold gate vpon hir xxxiij doughters eldest callid albyne damisels whan come vnto age bicome fair wōder wherfor dyoclisiā anon lete make somenyng cōmaūded lrēs kynges helden shold come certayn day lrēs conteyned make ryal feste whiche daye thider comen brought hem amyrals prynces duke noble chiualrye feste ryally awayed ther lyued ioye myrthe ynough wonder wyt befel thus dyoclisian thought marye doughters amonge alle tho kynges tho solēpnyte spaken dide albyne eldest doughter al hir sustres richely maried vnto xxxiij kynges lordes grece honour power solempnyte whan solempnite done euery kynge toke wyf lad hem owne coūtrey ther made hem quenes befel thus afterward dame albyne bycome stoute sterne told lytel pry lord hym scorne despyte wold done hys wyll wold haue hir owne wyll dyuerse mater hir sustres euerychone bere hem euyl ayenst hir lordes wonder wytte moch hem thought hir husbondes nought hye parage comen hir fader tho kynges hir lordes wold haue chastysed hem fayr speche behestes also yeftes warned hem fair maner vpon al loue frendship shold amende lither condicions al nought dyden owne wyll thynge hem lyked power wherfore tho xxxiij kynges vpon tyme oftymes beten theyr wynes wende wolde haue amended tatches hyr wicked thewes suche condicions fayre speche warnynge dydden al wers setynges •… one moche wers wherfor kyng wedded albyne wrote tatches condicions wyf albyn letter sent dioclisian fader whan kynges herd albynes lord sent letter dyoclisian anone sente lrēs ensealed hir seales condicions tatches hir wyues whan kyng dyoclisian saw herd many playntes doughters soore ashamed byoome wonder angry wroth towarde doughters thought nyght day yf myght tho amende mysdid anon sent letter vnto xxxiij kynges sholde come hym brynge hem wyues euerychone certayne daye wolde ther chastyse theyr wyckednes yf myght ony maner wyse soo kynges comen al daye tyme tho sette bitwene hem kyng dioclisian hem vnderfeng moche honour made solempne fest al vn der lorship thyrdde day solempnyte kyng dioclisian sent xxxiij doughters shold come speke hym chambre whan come spa •… vnto hem theyr wykkednesse cruelte despitously hem reproued vndernā said yf wold chasty sed shold loue lese euermore whan ladyes herd thie bycomen abasshed gretely ashamed fader said wold make al amendes departed hir faders chambre dame albyn eldest suster lad hem al hir chambre tho made wide al therin soo lyf amonges hem hir sustres fere tho said albyne fair sistres wel knowē king fader v hath reproued shamed despised enchesen make v obedyēt vnto oure husbondes certes shal neuer while lyue syth come hyer kynges blode myn husbonde whan thus sayd alle hir sustres said tho sayd albyne ful wel wote fair sustres husbondes haue pleyned vnto fader vpon v wherfor hath v thus fowlo reproued despysed wherfor susters coūseyl nyght husbondes ben bed al one assent cutten throtes may ben pee hem better may thys thyng vnder faders power elles anone al ladyes cō sented graūted counseyl whan nyght come lordes ladyes went bedde anone hyr lordes slepe cut al hir husbondes throtes slowen hem alle whan dioclosyan kyng fader herd thynge bycome hugely wroth ayenst doughters anone wolde hem al haue brente al baron lordes firrie coūseylled doo suche sternesse owne doughters shold wide land hem euermore neuer shold come ayene dyde dioclisyan fader anon commaūded hem goo ship delyuerd hem vytaylles half yere whan done alle sustren wente ship sayled forth see bytoke frendes appolyn hir god long saylled see til atte last come arryued yle al wil dernesse whanne dame albyne come londe hir sustres albyne went forth oute ship sayd hir sustres moche quod ol 〈◊〉 suster companye fyrst lande haue taken moche name albyne wyll lond callyd albyon myne owne name anone hir sustres graunted hyr good wyll tho went alle sustres ship token land albion hir suster callyd ther went vp downe fonde nether man ne woman ne child wild beestes dyuerse kyndes whan hyr vytayl le dyspended hem fayled fedde hem herbes frutes season yere soo lyued best myght toke flesshe dyuerse beestes bycame wonder fat desyred mannys companye mannys kynde hem faylled hete woxen wonder coragyous kynde desyred mannys company ony othir solace myrth whan deuyl perceyued went dyuerse countreys toke body eyr lykyng nature shad men •… e lande albyon laye tho wymmen shad tho nature vpon hem conceyued brought forth geantz whiche callyd one gogmagog another laugherigan named dyuerse name maner come forth borne horryble geants albyon dwellyd caues hilles wyll londe albyon hem liked vnto tyme brute arryued come totnesse yle albyon ther brute conquerd discomfyted geants aboue sayd 〈◊〉 endeth prologue albyon tho yle •… eneth brute goten slowe first moder afterward fader conquerd albyon named brytayn owne name called englond name engyst saxon ca j noble cyte grete troye ther noble knyght man grete power callyd eneas whan cyte troye lost destro yed thurgh hem grece encas alle meyne fled then come lombardye tho lord gouernour lond kyng cal led latyn another kyng ther callyd turocelyne strongly werrid vpon king latyn oftymes dyd hym moche harme whan kyng latyn herde eneas comen vnderfenge moche honoure hym helde moch herd hym wist wel noble knyght worthy body dedes ene helpe kyng latyn werre shortly telle well worthyly dyd slowe turocelyne discomfyted hym peple whan done kyng latyn yaf al lond turecelinis eneas maryage lauyne doughter moost fayr crature ony man wyst lyued geder io •… murthe hir lyfes tyme wed ded wyf vpon hir bygate sone callyd silueyne silueyne whan coude reson man vnwyting fader ageynst acqueynted damisel cosyn lauyne kyng latynes doughter quene eneas wyf brought damysel child whan ascamus fader wyste anon lete enquere wysest maistres grettest clerkes child damisel shol de bringe forth ansuerd said shold bryng forth sone shold slee fader moder dyd mo der dyed beryng hym whan child born fader le •… e calle hym brute maystres sayd shold moche harme sorow many dyuerse place shold co grete honour worship kyng ascam •… deyde whan god wold silueyne sone receyued lande made hym derlych wel byloued among peple whan brute silueynus sone xv yere olde went vpon daye fadre play solace brute shold shete vnto hert arowe myshapped glaced brute quelled fader brute dryuen oute lande helde hym grece ca ij whan myschance befalle peple lāde made sorwe ynow sore angred encheson therof dryuen brute lond wold suffre hym amongys hem saugh muste abyde wente fro thēs grece fonde vij 〈◊〉 mē linage kynred troye comen grete blode storye tellyth men woman childeren whiche alle holden thraldome bondage kynge pandras grece deth achilles bitraid slayne troye brute wonder fayre man stronge huge age glad chere semblaunt also worthy body wel beloued among people kynge pandras herde speke goodnes condicions anone made hym duelle soo brute bycome wōder priue moche beloued kyng long tyme brute duelled kyng soo last troye brute spaken geder kynred lignage acqueyntaūce ther pleyned hem vnto brute hir sorowe hir bondage many shame kyng paudras hem done brute saiden vpon tyme ye lord lignage strong man myghty ye capitayn lord wylle bycome men cōmandementz done al manere thynges brynge ye v oute wrecchednesse bondage fyght kyng thorugh grace grete god shal hym ouercome shal make kynge lond done homage yow shul holde euermore brute tho grete pyte hyr bondage broughte preuelich went hym kynges court al tho troye went put hem wodes montaygnes hem helde sente vnto kynge pandras shold yeue hem leue sauelych wend land nold lenger duelle bondage kyng pandras tho sore noyed tho swore wold slee hem euerychone ordeined grete power went towardes hem al fight brute men manlyche hem defended fyersly foughten slewe kynges men none hem escaped token kyng hym helde pryson ordeyned coūceyll bytwene hem myght done sayd shold put deth somme sayd shold exyled lande somme sayd shold 〈◊〉 tho spak wyse knyght called memprys sayd bru •… al tho tooye yf kyn •… pand •… wolde yelde hym haue lyf counseylle yeue vnto brute duke soueraygne doughter gennogen wyfe maryage honderd shippes wel arayd alle tresoure gold siluer corne wyn moche v nedeth haue one thyng goo oute land ordeyne v lande elleswher ne none kynred comen v shal neuer haue pee lande amōges hem grece haue slayne many hyr knyghtes frendes euermore warre contake shold bene amonges v brute tho folke consentyd well counseylle thyng tolden kyng pandras therfor haue hys lyf graunted moche axed anone yaf vnto brute gennogen doughter wif honderd shippis moche hem neded vitayllis ordeyned bru te tho toke wyf men forsoke land gre ce wenten hem vnto see hadden wynde weder wy comen thyrdde day yle callyd •… g •… brute anon sente men londe aspye maner contre founden old cyte al wasted forlet na •… theryn nether man ne woman ne thyng duellyng myddel cyte foūden old temple fayre lady thas callyd dyane goddesse comen ayene vn brute told hym seen founden counceylled hym gone doo sacryfyce vnto dame diane woned yeue answer thyng euer men prayde namely vn honoured sacrifice brute went ymage said diane noble goddesse lady al thyng hast myght thy power wyn de wat •… wodes feldes alle thynges world alle maner beestes ther westmer good man worthy body wel gouerned lande hit befell tydyng ca hym day kyng roderick gascoyne come land huge nombre pe ple duellyng staynesmore whan kynge westmer herde tho tydynges leete as •… bled hem went seche alured tho new kyng southsex ther founde hym wyltone lytel pe ple netheles fought hem atte last fled then felde wente westsexe ordeyned soo moche people owne royamme also soo tyll strong hoost danoys power ageynst hym stonde come london hooste ther dane soiourned ther wold haue foughten hem dane durst hym▪ fighten praid hym pee muste gone ageyne hir owne countrry neuermore englond come ageyne ony harme done vpon couenaunt shold yeue hym pledge good hostage suche englysshmen wold axen hubba hungar slayn chippenham howe danoys brought hyr kyng kyng cao c viijo daye danoys departed london soo fast riden nyght day neuer toke rest goyng til comen vnto excetre toke tho toune helde hem whan kynge alured herd tydyng anone lete take hostage went then excestre power whan danoys herde alle co myng wenten fro then westsex come shippenam ther dyden moche harme countre robbed folke brought hem prison kyng alured hem pursiewed come vpon hem fyersly hem assaylled slayne hubba hungar broder buerne bocard bataylle moche folke slayne one partye gore felde left danoys moch kyng tho come lytel company kyng hasted hym moche myght wende ayene whan danoys founden hubba body lyggyng dede entered made vpon grete lodge lete calle hubbeslowe called daye place deuenshyre baron somersete wylteshyre dorsete herd telle hir king discōfyted ordeyned al power myghten haue come kyng ther thanked god hadde hym founde alyue went danoys hym slayn tho toke counceyll kyng baron wold gone seche dane hem fyghten ryden al nyght hem seche comen morow prime abingdon ther danoys kyng tho alured baron assembled ther assaylled dane egrely yaf hem strōg batail dane nobly put hem long time man wist whether partye peple slayne thus befelle god wold kynge alured hadde vyctorye wyth moche honour daneys dryuen ne wyst whyder torne xv dayes kyng hem pursued wil glad fayne speken pee accord token hym good hostage sayd wolde neuer vpon hym werre ne none debate arere ouer lehiht kyng englond haue ageyne al hir landes hir rentrs wold make restitucion goodes taken hir ageynst hir wylle kynge self tho pandulfe erles baron went tho vnto wynchestre ageynst arcwbis shop stephen whan come kyng went ageynst hym fell doune foot said hym fair syre ye welcome crye yow mercy encheson haue trespaced ayenst yowe archebisshop toke hym vp tho armes kyssed hym curoysly oftymes lad hym dore seynt swythynes chirche honde assoylled hym sentence hym reconciled god holy chirche seynt margarets day archebisshop anon went synge masse leyng offred masse marc gold whan masse done al wente vnderfonge alle hyr landes withoute ony maner gayn sayeng day made myrth ioye ynough yet enterdytyng rele ced encheson pope set enterdyting shold vndone til kyng made ful restituciō goodes take holy chirch also hym self shold done homage pope certayne legate shold sende englond tho toke pandolfe leue kyng archebisshop went ageyne vnto rome archebisshop anone let come hym prelate holy chirche letter shold paye iulyane yelde ageyne kynge rychardes wyf thyrd parte land englond irlond witholde syth kyng rychard deyde whan kyng iohan herd wonder wroth vtterlych enterdytyng myght ben vndone broken wold noo lawe holde dyd thyng hym lyked dysheryted many men oute consente lordes perys land wold disherite good erle randulf erle chestre encheson vndertoke hym wykkednes cause dyd moche shame ashamed lytel company hym dyscomfyted shamelyche put hym al company alyue flee tho come sir edward bayllol toke countray aboute hym till come vnto abbay dunfermelyne ther founde vytaylles hym folke among al thynges fonde chambre aboute v honderd grete staues fyne oke longe pykes yren stele toke hem delyuerd hem moost strengest men companye anone wente fro then lodged hym felde ij myle saynt iohannes toune whan burgeis tonne herde erle fyffe discomfyted thurgh bayllol sore adrad breken theyr brydges made ouer water erue bayllol myght gone ouer wherfor lodged hym nyght litel hede toke reste sayd vnto peple nowe dere lordes ye knowe ful wel lodged bytwene enemyes yf mowe v hampre ther bote deth wherfor yf abyde al nyghte stylle leue shal torne v moche sorow harme power scotland may euery day weye encrease may done ben lytel peple ayenst hem wherfor pray yow loue almyghty god make v bold hardy maye myghtely take scottes nyght boldely werre vpon hem lete v pursue hem nyght yf trauaylled thurgh v see hardynesse scottes comen mete hem see hem trauaylled wery sorer wyll adrad v fyght fiersly shal fyght hem vpon hem pursue soo thurgh grace god amyghty alle world shal speke doughtnes chyualrye sir vnderstondeth wel al company comen sir edward bayllol graunted wel vnto counceyll ther glad anon pursued vpon scottes byco wonder wery bayllol companye sore folowed hem dyd hem moche sorow thurgh hyr assaute myght feble hem helpe lytell peple tho sayd scottes amonges hem byfal li cell peple bayllol hath wynge done v moch traua ylle sorowe nowe certes semeth v worcheth grace wonder gracious quarell al certes shal ben dede may come hym v yelde sith fadre set v pry among thynges bayllol peple passed water erue syre rogyer swynerton sone fyers angry went forth saw peple armes ful well arayed forth wente vn hem hem foughten slewe many wold abyde toke netheles assaute wende hadde grete hoost scotland whan come morne gadred hem geder rested hem whrle whyle eglysshmen rested hem noble baron thomas vesey noble baron stafford pril •… ed hir lo •… vp doune hylles kepe estres countrey pryked vp doune saw grete hoost good aray ordeyned thre wynges helmes sheldes shynyng co myng vpon hem tho come tho two lordes ayene vnto baillols folke sayd loue almyghty god ben good cō fort ye shal haue batayll anon ryght tho spake sir fouke sone gareyne baron grete renōme dede ar me syres lordynges vnderstondeth wylle saye haue seyn many dyuerse wynges wel amōge sarazyns iewee among scottes yet saw neuer ferth part wyn ge fyght therfor yf wil abyde enemyes ynowe fyght ayenst hem yf good hert good wyl late v fyght hem certes ben ful •… n company therfor loue god take vnto v good hert lete v ben bold thenke nether wy ues ne child onlyche conquere hem batayl thurgh helpe lord god enemyes shal ouercome come hoost scottes towardes hem ful fie sly ayenst syr edward bayllol thre bataylles well arayed armure wonder syerly come toward bayllols men whan syre donald erle marall sawe al sayd robert buts sone robert brus wordes syr robert quod ful sore forthynketh ne hert folk baillol brouȝt hym shold dye dynt scottissh swerd sith yt ben cristen men wel ben therfor thynketh grete charite send vnto hem yeld hem vnto mercy grace raunsonne hem thurgh greuous raunsonne moche haue taken land done ylle certes quod sir robert brus haue wel perceyued thou art enemye trai tour vnto scotland sith thou wylt consent saue dedely enemyes haue done v moche sorow shame semeth wel ye ben hir assent certes robert quod syre donald falsely ye lye hir company ne hir consent hastely ye shal see wylle fyght hem rather ony company certes syr robert sayd shal maugre thyn hede assaylle hem er thou prike ten hir stedes fiersly vpon caskemore hyr wenges fole wrd venge tho come met baillol cōpa nye hongyng bought streit passage fast hasted hem vnto englysshmen thousandes fell groūde eche vp hepe hors man baillol tho men myghtely stode ayenst hem fast slewe scottes vnto groūde many sore wounded long til stoden vpon hem feined hem hir swerdes speres thurgh bodyes sore trauailled vpon hem til bioomen ful wery wist done scottes left ali ue fledden wey saue hem self best man myȝt tho pursued hem sir edward bayllol men slewe hem til nyȝt fro then went vnto seynt iohans toun toke held hem vitaylled hem self hir owne foūden ynowe wherwith make hem mery tho made bayllol men woūded gone shippe wēde englōd hele hyr woūdes time ther flemmyng see strong robber callyd crabbe flemmynge dryuen oute flaundres wykkednes therfor come scotland holde scottes dyde moche harme vnto englysshmen myght crabbe met see bayllols men wounded batayll sente ayene englond hele hir woundes crabbe yafe vnto hem grete assaute wold haue slayn hem eueryeho ne englysshmen defended hem wel manly discō fited crabbe companye tho gone flee scot land come toward saynt iohans toune foūd gre te company scottes comen ageyn geder dy scomfiture gaskemore whiche besyeged bayllol mē toune saynt iohan anon told scottes discomfyted englysshmen woūded gaskemore went toward englond hele woūdes sayd scottes shold haue myghte ne grace ageynst edward bayllol encheson scomfyted empeired chyualrye scotland handeful men ac compt ageynst scottes slayne wherfor coū ceilled remeue fiege saynt iohans toun kepe hem best maner coude myght scottes vnderstode tho crabbe sayd hem soth forsoke siege went then nyght halpe hem self best maner miȝt whan thynge knowe thurgh scotland lordes knyghtes scomfyted gaskemore scotland thurgh sir edward bayllol ye shal vnderstonde lor de ladyes gentils scotland comen wonder fast saynt iohanes toun yelde hem vnto bayllol hym dyden homage feaute hir landes yelden hem pee hem resceyued frely fro then went abbey scone ther crouned kynge scotland lete crye pee thurgh oute al land tyme bifell kyng edward helde parlement amōg lyeges newe castel vp tyne amende trespa ce wronges done land sir edward bayllol kyng scotland come hym thyder dyd hym seante homage reame scotland maner kyng edward englond gadred ageyne homage fe autes scotland wherof put thurgh counceyll assent dame isabell moder sir rog •… er mortimer erle marche
